   protected Map<Node, FetchSessionHandler.FetchRequestData> prepareFetchRequests() {\n        // Update metrics in case there was an assignment change\n        metricsManager.maybeUpdateAssignment(subscriptions);\n\n        Map<Node, FetchSessionHandler.Builder> fetchable = new HashMap<>();\n        long currentTimeMs = time.milliseconds();\n        Map<String, Uuid> topicIds = metadata.topicIds();\n\n        // This is the set of partitions that have buffered data\n        Set<TopicPartition> buffered = Collections.unmodifiableSet(fetchBuffer.bufferedPartitions());\n\n        // This is the set of partitions that do not have buffered data\n        Set<TopicPartition> unbuffered = fetchablePartitions(buffered);\n\n        if (unbuffered.isEmpty()) {\n            // If there are no partitions that don't already have data locally buffered, there's no need to issue\n            // any fetch requests at the present time.\n            return Collections.emptyMap();\n        }\n\n        Set<Integer> bufferedNodes = bufferedNodes(buffered, currentTimeMs);\n\n        for (TopicPartition partition : unbuffered) {\n            SubscriptionState.FetchPosition position = positionForPartition(partition);\n            Optional<Node> nodeOpt = maybeNodeForPosition(partition, position, currentTimeMs);\n\n            if (nodeOpt.isEmpty())\n                continue;\n\n            Node node = nodeOpt.get();\n\n            if (isUnavailable(node)) {\n                maybeThrowAuthFailure(node);\n\n                // If we try to send during the reconnect backoff window, then the request is just\n                // going to be failed anyway before being sent, so skip sending the request for now\n                log.trace(\"Skipping fetch for partition {} because node {} is awaiting reconnect backoff\", partition, node);\n            } else if (nodesWithPendingFetchRequests.contains(node.id())) {\n                // If there's already an inflight request for this node, don't issue another request.\n                log.trace(\"Skipping fetch for partition {} because previous request to {} has not been processed\", partition, node);\n            } else if (bufferedNodes.contains(node.id())) {\n                // While a node has buffered data, don't fetch other partition data from it. Because the buffered\n                // partitions are not included in the fetch request, those partitions will be inadvertently dropped\n                // from the broker fetch session cache. In some cases, that could lead to the entire fetch session\n                // being evicted.\n                log.trace(\"Skipping fetch for partition {} because its leader node {} hosts buffered partitions\", partition, node);\n            } else {\n                // if there is a leader and no in-flight requests, issue a new fetch\n                FetchSessionHandler.Builder builder = fetchable.computeIfAbsent(node, k -> {\n                    FetchSessionHandler fetchSessionHandler = sessionHandlers.computeIfAbsent(node.id(), n -> new FetchSessionHandler(logContext, n));\n                    return fetchSessionHandler.newBuilder();\n                });\n                Uuid topicId = topicIds.getOrDefault(partition.topic(), Uuid.ZERO_UUID);\n                FetchRequest.PartitionData partitionData = new FetchRequest.PartitionData(topicId,\n                        position.offset,\n                        FetchRequest.INVALID_LOG_START_OFFSET,\n                        fetchConfig.fetchSize,\n                        position.currentLeader.epoch,\n                        Optional.empty());\n                builder.add(partition, partitionData);\n\n                log.debug(\"Added {} fetch request for partition {} at position {} to node {}\", fetchConfig.isolationLevel,\n                        partition, position, node);\n            }\n        }\n\n        return convert(fetchable);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * This method converts {@link FetchSessionHandler.Builder} instances to\n     * {@link FetchSessionHandler.FetchRequestData} instances. See the exception for more details\n     * @throws org.apache.kafka.common.KafkaException for any other unrecoverable errors (e.g. if offset metadata\n     *             is too large or if the topic does not exist).\n     * @throws org.apache.kafka.common.errors.TimeoutException if the timeout expires before successful completion\n     *            of the offset commit\n     * @throws org.apache.kafka.common.errors.FencedInstanceIdException if this consumer is using the classic group protocol\n     *            and this instance gets fenced by broker.\n     */\n    @Override\n    public void commitSync(Duration timeout) {\n        delegate.commitSync(timeout);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Commit the specified offsets for the specified list of topics and partitions.\n     * <p>\n     * This commits offsets to Kafka. REQUEST BUILDING PHASE:\\n   - Fetcher.sendFetchesInternal() calls AbstractFetch.prepareFetchRequests() (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/AbstractFetch.java:412) to prepare fetch requests for all fetchable partitions organized by node.\\n   - prepareFetchRequests() builds a FetchSessionHandler.Builder for each node and creates FetchRequest.PartitionData for each partition.\\n   - For each node, AbstractFetch.createFetchRequest(Node, FetchSessionHandler.FetchRequestData) (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/AbstractFetch.java:301) constructs a FetchRequest.Builder using FetchRequest.Builder.forConsumer() (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/FetchRequest.java:166).\\n   - The builder configures isolation level, max bytes, metadata, and removed/replaced partitions before being sent via client.send().\\n\\n4. NETWORK TRANSMISSION:\\n   - Fetcher.sendFetchesInternal() sends the built FetchRequest.Builder to the network client and registers response listeners.\\n   - For asynchronous handling, FetchRequestManager follows a similar pattern via FetchRequestManager.poll() and FetchRequestManager.pollInternal() (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/FetchRequestManager.java:103, 137).\\n\\n5. RESPONSE PARSING PHASE:\\n   - Upon receiving the response, AbstractFetch.handleFetchSuccess(Node, FetchSessionHandler.FetchRequestData, ClientResponse) (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/AbstractFetch.java:150) is invoked.\\n   - handleFetchSuccess() extracts the FetchResponse from the ClientResponse and calls FetchResponse.responseData(Map<Uuid, String>, short) (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/FetchResponse.java:98) to parse partition data and topic IDs.\\n   - For each partition, a CompletedFetch is created with the FetchResponseData.PartitionData and added to the FetchBuffer.\\n\\n6. RECORD EXTRACTION AND DESERIALIZATION:\\n   - ClassicKafkaConsumer.pollForFetches() calls Fetcher.collectFetch() (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/Fetcher.java:145) which delegates to FetchCollector.collectFetch(FetchBuffer) (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/FetchCollector.java:92).\\n   - FetchCollector.collectFetch() iterates through completed fetches and calls FetchCollector.fetchRecords(CompletedFetch, int) (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/FetchCollector.java:150) for each partition.\\n   - FetchCollector.fetchRecords() calls CompletedFetch.fetchRecords(FetchConfig, Deserializers, int) (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/CompletedFetch.java:252) to extract and deserialize records from record batches.\\n   - CompletedFetch.fetchRecords() iterates through batches, calls CompletedFetch.parseRecord(Deserializers, TopicPartition, Optional<Integer>, TimestampType, Record) (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/CompletedFetch.java:307) for each record to deserialize key/value and create ConsumerRecord objects.\\n\\n7. FETCH AGGREGATION:\\n   - FetchCollector.fetchRecords() wraps the extracted records in a Fetch object via Fetch.forPartition(TopicPartition, List<ConsumerRecord>, boolean, OffsetAndMetadata) (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/Fetch.java:43).\\n   - Multiple Fetch objects from different partitions are aggregated together.\\n\\n8.
